## Effects for habitable conversion engine which runs in event atw_engine.01

# SUPER-TERRESTRIAL CLASSES

roll_chloerosgaean = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	# Spawn new class modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_chloerosgaean" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-artificial" days = -1 }
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	# Update texture/portrait	
	add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-seeded" days = -1 }
	
	set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	random_list = {
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "biome_chloerosgaean"
				entity = "super_terrestrial_chloerosgaean_01_entity"
				
			}
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_chloerosgaean"
				entity = "super_terrestrial_chloerosgaean_01_entity"
				
			}
		}
	}
	# Replace Mars entity
	if = {
		limit = { has_planet_flag = "planet_mars" }
		set_planet_entity = {
			entity = "super_terrestrial_chloerosgaean_mars_01_entity"			
		}
	}
	# Replace Earth entity
	if = {
		limit = { has_planet_flag = "planet_earth" }
		set_planet_entity = {
			entity = "super_terrestrial_chloerosgaean_earth_01_entity"			
		}
	}
}

# TERRESTRIAL CLASSES

roll_chloerosorimos = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	# Spawn new class modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_chloerosorimos" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	spawn_atmosphere-chloerosorimos = yes
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	# Homeworlds must roll the default biosphere
	if = {
		limit = { is_homeworld = yes }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
		# Update texture/portrait
		
		set_planet_entity = {
			picture = "biome_chloerosorimos_diverse"
			entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_diverse_01_entity"
			
		}
		set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	}
	# If not, randomize the biosphere with the proper texture
	else = {
		spawn_biosphere = yes
		random_list = {
			0 = {	# Roll with Dense biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_chloerosorimos_dense"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_dense_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_chloerosorimos"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_dense_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Diverse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_chloerosorimos_diverse"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_chloerosorimos"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse"				
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Sparse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_chloerosorimos_sparse"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_chloerosorimos"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosorimos_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse"
			}
		}
	}	
}

roll_chloerosgenian = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	# Spawn new class modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_chloerosgenian" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	spawn_atmosphere-chloerosgenian = yes
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	# Homeworlds must roll the default biosphere
	if = {
		limit = { is_homeworld = yes }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
		# Update texture/portrait		
		set_planet_entity = {
			picture = "biome_chloerosgenian_diverse"
			entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_diverse_01_entity"
			
		}
		set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	}
	# If not, randomize the biosphere with the proper texture
	else = {
		spawn_biosphere = yes
		random_list = {
			0 = {	# Roll with Dense biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_chloerosgenian_dense"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_dense_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_chloerosgenian"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_dense_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Diverse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_chloerosgenian_diverse"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_chloerosgenian"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Sparse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_chloerosgenian_sparse"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_sparse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_chloerosgenian"
							entity = "terrestrial_chloerosgenian_sparse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse"
			}
		}
	}	
}

roll_xirosorimos = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	# Spawn new class modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_xirosorimos" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	spawn_atmosphere-xirosorimos = yes
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	# Homeworlds must roll the default biosphere

		limit = { is_homeworld = yes }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
		# Update texture/portrait
		set_planet_entity = {
			picture = "biome_xirosorimos_sparse"
			entity = "terrestrial_xirosorimos_sparse_01_entity"
			
		}
		set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	}
	# If not, randomize the biosphere with the proper texture

		spawn_biosphere = yes
		random_list = {
			0 = {	# Roll with Diverse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }

					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_xirosorimos_diverse"
							entity = "terrestrial_xirosorimos_sparse_01_entity"

					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_xirosorimos"
							entity = "terrestrial_xirosorimos_sparse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Tenuous biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }

				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }

				random_list = {

roll_thermogenian = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	# Spawn new class modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_thermogenian" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	spawn_atmosphere-thermogenian = yes
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	# Homeworlds must roll the default biosphere
	if = {
		limit = { is_homeworld = yes }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-tenuous" days = -1 }
		# Update texture/portrait
		set_planet_entity = {
			picture = "biome_thermogenian_tenuous"
			entity = "terrestrial_thermogenian_barren_01_entity"
			
		}
		set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	}
	# If not, randomize the biosphere with the proper texture
	else = {
		spawn_biosphere = yes
		random_list = {
			0 = {	# Roll with Diverse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }

					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_thermogenian_diverse"
							entity = "terrestrial_thermogenian_diverse_01_entity"

					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait

							picture = "orbit_thermogenian"
							entity = "terrestrial_thermogenian_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}

				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }

				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }

						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_thermogenian_sparse"

					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_thermogenian"
							entity = "terrestrial_thermogenian_sparse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Tenuous biosphere

# SUB-TERRESTRIAL CLASSES

roll_tropikostopio = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	# Spawn new class modifier
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_tropikostopio" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	spawn_atmosphere-tropikostopio = yes
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	# Homeworlds must roll the default biosphere
	if = {
		limit = { is_homeworld = yes }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
		# Update texture/portrait
		set_planet_entity = {
			picture = "biome_tropikostopio_dense"
			entity = "sub_terrestrial_tropikostopio_dense_01_entity"
			
		}
		set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	}
	# If not, randomize the biosphere with the proper texture
	else = {
		spawn_biosphere = yes
		random_list = {
			0 = {	# Roll with Dense biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_tropikostopio_dense"
							entity = "sub_terrestrial_tropikostopio_dense_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_tropikostopio"
							entity = "sub_terrestrial_tropikostopio_dense_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Diverse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_tropikostopio_diverse"
							entity = "sub_terrestrial_tropikostopio_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_tropikostopio"
							entity = "sub_terrestrial_tropikostopio_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}

	# Homeworlds must roll the default biosphere
	if = {
		limit = { is_homeworld = yes }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
		# Update texture/portrait
		set_planet_entity = {
			picture = "biome_ipeirospelagic_sparse"
			entity = "oceanic_ipeirospelagic_diverse_01_entity"
			
		}
		set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
	}
	# If not, randomize the biosphere with the proper texture
	else = {
		spawn_biosphere = yes
		random_list = {
			0 = {	# Roll with Sparse biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_ipeirospelagic_sparse"
							entity = "oceanic_ipeirospelagic_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_ipeirospelagicn"
							entity = "oceanic_ipeirospelagic_diverse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse"
			}
			0 = {	# Roll with Tenuous biosphere
				# Base modifier
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse" }
				modifier = { add = 10 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous" }
				modifier = { add = 0 has_planet_flag = "biosphere-barren" }
				
				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-tenuous" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_ipeirospelagic_tenuous"
							entity = "oceanic_ipeirospelagic_sparse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_ipeirospelagic"
							entity = "oceanic_ipeirospelagic_sparse_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"

				add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-barren" days = -1 }
				# Update texture/portrait
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = yes } # Colonized worlds will use biome portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "biome_pagospelagic_barren"
							entity = "oceanic_pagospelagic_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
					0 = {
						modifier = { add = 10 is_colony = no } # Uncolonized worlds will use orbit portrait
						set_planet_entity = {
							picture = "orbit_pagospelagic"
							entity = "oceanic_pagospelagic_01_entity"
							
						}
					}
				}
				set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
				remove_planet_flag = "biosphere-tenuous"
			}
		}
	}
}

roll_xiroslykofos = {
	# These planets are rare enough, we should always convert, unless there is already another tidally-locked in the system
	random_list = {
		100 = {
			# Skip conversion and let the planet remain an uninhabitable class
			remove_planet_flag = "locked_hot"
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			# Roll a Hothouse instead
			clear_deposits = yes
			change_pc = "pc_toxic"
			roll_hothouse_toxic = yes
			# We still need the flag habitable_converted to make sure the process does not repeat
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
			 # Increase the odds significantly of skipping conversion if there is already another tidally-locked planet rolled in the system
			 modifier = { factor = 10.00 solar_system = { any_system_planet = { has_planet_flag = "tidal_rolled" } } }
		}
		10 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes			
			# Roll a Tidally-locked habitable planet
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_xiroslykofos" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_savannah
			reroll_deposits = yes
			spawn_atmosphere-xiroslykofos = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_xiroslykofos"
				entity = "tidal_xiroslykofos_01_entity"
				
			}
			
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
			set_planet_flag = "tidal_rolled"
			# Increase the odds of converting if there is no other valid tidally-locked planet in the system for converting
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 solar_system = { any_system_planet = { NOR = { has_planet_flag = "locked_temperate" has_planet_flag = "locked_cold" } } } }
			# Extra modifier based on the habitable scale picked in the game settings
			complex_trigger_modifier = {
				trigger = check_galaxy_setup_value
				parameters = {
					setting = habitable_worlds_scale
				}
				mode = factor
			}
		}
	}
}

roll_primordial = {
	# These planets are rare enough, they should have higher odds of conversion, unless there is already another type of habitable in the system
	random_list = {
		2 = {
			# Skip conversion and let the planet remain an uninhabitable class
			remove_planet_flag = "primordial"
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes
			# Roll a Volcanic world instead
			clear_deposits = yes
			change_pc = "pc_barren"
			roll_volcanic_telluric = yes
			# We still need the flag habitable_converted to make sure the process does not repeat
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
			# Increase the odds significantly of skipping conversion if there is another habitable in the system already
			modifier = { factor = 10.00 solar_system = { any_system_planet = { is_habitable = yes } } }
			# Lower the odds of skipping if it is flagged as forced
			modifier = { factor = 0.00 has_planet_flag = "forced" }
		}
		10 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes
			# Roll a Hadean class

			change_pc = pc_molten
			clear_deposits = yes

			set_planet_flag = "marginal_converted"

			complex_trigger_modifier = {

roll_liquid_water = {
	# Higher chance of getting a marginal world if there is a standard habitable world, so the marginal may be used as a system colony
	random_list = {
		30 = {
			# Skip conversion and let the planet remain an uninhabitable class
			remove_planet_flag = "liquid_water"
			# We still need the flag habitable_converted to make sure the process does not repeat
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
			# Increase the odds significantly of skipping conversion if there is another habitable in the system already
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 solar_system = { any_system_planet = { is_habitable = yes } } }
			modifier = { factor = 10.00 solar_system = { any_system_planet = { has_planet_flag = "marginal_converted" } } }
			# Lower the odds of skipping if it is flagged as forced
			modifier = { factor = 0.00 has_planet_flag = "forced" }
		}
		10 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes
			# Roll an Agonos class
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_agonos" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_barren
			clear_deposits = yes
			spawn_atmosphere-agonos = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_agonos"
				entity = "marginal_agonos_01_entity"
				
			}
			#add_modifier = { modifier = "terraforming_candidate" days = -1 }
			set_planet_flag = "marginal_converted"
			# Modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 NOT = { orbits_hot_star = yes } }
			# Extra modifier based on the habitable scale picked in the game settings
			complex_trigger_modifier = {
				trigger = check_galaxy_setup_value
				parameters = {
					setting = habitable_worlds_scale
				}
				mode = factor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.00
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "toxic_terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "frozen_terraforming_candidate"
				}
			}
		}
		10 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes
			# Roll an Elos class

				trigger = check_galaxy_setup_value
				parameters = {
					setting = habitable_worlds_scale
				}
				mode = factor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.00
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "toxic_terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "frozen_terraforming_candidate"
				}
			}
		}
		10 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes

			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_alkali" days = -1 }

				trigger = check_galaxy_setup_value
				parameters = {
					setting = habitable_worlds_scale
				}
				mode = factor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.00
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "toxic_terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "frozen_terraforming_candidate"
				}
			}
		}
		10 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes
			# Roll a Redux class			
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_redux" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_toxic
			clear_deposits = yes
			spawn_atmosphere-redux = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_redux"
				entity = "sub_marginal_redux_01_entity"
				
			}
			#add_modifier = { modifier = "terraforming_candidate" days = -1 }
			set_planet_flag = "marginal_converted"
			# Modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 NOT = { is_moon = yes } }
			# Extra modifier based on the habitable scale picked in the game settings
			complex_trigger_modifier = {
				trigger = check_galaxy_setup_value
				parameters = {
					setting = habitable_worlds_scale
				}
				mode = factor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.00
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "toxic_terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "frozen_terraforming_candidate"
				}
			}
		}
		15 = {
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = yes
			# Roll an Ammoniapelagic class
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_ammoniapelagic" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_ocean
			reroll_deposits = yes
			spawn_atmosphere-ammoniapelagic = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-ammonia" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_ammoniapelagic"
				entity = "ammonia_panthalassic_planet_01_entity"
				
			}
			#add_modifier = { modifier = "terraforming_candidate" days = -1 }
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
			correct_habitable_deposits = yes
			# Modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 NOT = { is_gas_giant_moon = yes } }
			# Extra modifier based on the habitable scale picked in the game settings
			complex_trigger_modifier = {
				trigger = check_galaxy_setup_value
				parameters = {
					setting = habitable_worlds_scale
				}
				mode = factor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.00
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "toxic_terraforming_candidate"
					has_modifier = "frozen_terraforming_candidate"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## ORIGIN CASES

roll_bioluminescent_origin = {
	# Remove previously spawned modifiers
	remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
	remove_class_modifier = yes
	add_modifier = { modifier = "class_photosgenian" days = -1 }
	# Spawn atomosphere modifier
	spawn_atmosphere-photosgenian = yes
	correct_atmosphere_color = yes
	add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
	# Update texture/portrait
	
	set_planet_entity = {
		picture = "biome_photosgenian"
		entity = "terrestrial_photosgenian_01_entity"
		
	}
	set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
}

roll_tidally_locked_origin = {
	random_list = {
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 1 has_climate = wet }
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			# Roll a Tidally-locked habitable planet
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_chloeroslykofos" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_tropical
			reroll_deposits = yes
			spawn_atmosphere-chloeroslykofos = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "biome_chloeroslykofos"
				entity = "tidal_chloeroslykofos_01_entity"
				
			}
			
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 1 has_climate = dry }
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			# Roll a Tidally-locked habitable planet
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_xiroslykofos" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_savannah
			reroll_deposits = yes
			spawn_atmosphere-xiroslykofos = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "biome_xiroslykofos"
				entity = "tidal_xiroslykofos_01_entity"
				
			}
			
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 1 has_climate = cold }
			# Remove previously spawned modifiers
			remove_atmosphere_modifier = yes
			remove_class_modifier = yes
			# Roll a Tidally-locked habitable planet
			add_modifier = { modifier = "class_pagoslykofos" days = -1 }
			change_pc = pc_alpine
			reroll_deposits = yes
			change_pc = pc_ocean
			spawn_atmosphere-pagoslykofos = yes
			correct_atmosphere_color = yes
			add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-aquatic" days = -1 }
			set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "biome_panpelagic_temperate"
				entity = "tidal_pagoslykofos_01_entity"
				
			}
			
			set_planet_flag = "habitable_converted"
		}
	}
}

# Effects to check if a planet has missing or wrong class
atw_habitable_check = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_gaia"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_chloerosgaean"
				has_modifier = "class_thermogaean"
				has_modifier = "class_cryogaean"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll one of the Gaia classes factoring its deposits
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				#modifier = { add = 100 orbits_ideal_star = yes }
				modifier = { add = 100 has_deposit = "d_lush_jungle" }
				modifier = { add = 100 has_deposit = "d_fertile_lands" }
				modifier = { add = 1000 has_deposit = "d_crystal_reef" }
				roll_chloerosgaean = yes
			}
			0 = {
				#modifier = { add = 100 orbits_hot_star = yes }
				modifier = { add = 100 has_deposit = "d_searing_desert" }
				modifier = { add = 100 has_deposit = "d_prosperous_mesa" }
				modifier = { add = 1000 has_deposit = "d_dust_desert" }
				roll_thermogaean = yes
			}
			0 = {
				#modifier = { add = 100 orbits_red_star = yes }
				modifier = { add = 100 has_deposit = "d_frozen_gas_lake" }
				modifier = { add = 100 has_deposit = "d_ore_rich_caverns" }
				modifier = { add = 1000 has_deposit = "d_fuming_bog" }
				roll_cryogaean = yes
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_relic"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOT = {
				has_planet_flag = habitable_converted
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_relic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_city"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOT = {
				has_planet_flag = habitable_converted
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_city = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_nuked"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_stepikos"
				has_modifier = "class_erimos"
				has_modifier = "class_karstikos"
				has_modifier = "class_agonos"
				has_modifier = "class_almyros"
				has_modifier = "class_elos"
				has_modifier = "class_hadean"
				has_modifier = "class_anthracean"
				has_modifier = "class_archean"
				has_modifier = "class_desolate"
				has_modifier = "class_hydrocarbonal"
				has_modifier = "class_alkali"
				has_modifier = "class_sulfuric"
				has_modifier = "class_ammoniagenian"
				has_modifier = "class_redux"
				has_modifier = "class_tomb"
				has_modifier = "class_tomb_restored"
				has_modifier = "class_barren_terraformed"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_tomb = yes
		reroll_planet = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_nuked"
			has_modifier = "biosphere-sparse"
			NOT = { has_modifier = "class_tomb_restored" }
		}
		remove_class_modifier = yes
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = "class_tomb_restored"
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_desert"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_thermopelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_ipeirospelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_aquatic_terraformed"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_thermopelagic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_arid"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_thermogenian"
				has_modifier = "class_xirosorimos"
				has_modifier = "class_mukesgenian"
				has_modifier = "class_algaemegagi"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_xirosorimos = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_savannah"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_thermotopio"
				has_modifier = "class_savana"
				has_modifier = "class_thermomegagi"
				has_modifier = "class_xiroslykofos"
				has_modifier = "class_adapted_terraformed"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_savana = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_continental"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_chloerosorimos"
				has_modifier = "class_chloerosgenian"
				has_modifier = "class_retinalgenian"
				has_modifier = "class_photosgenian"
				has_modifier = "class_megachlorida"
				has_modifier = "class_protogenian"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_chloerosorimos = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_tropical"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_tropikostopio"
				has_modifier = "class_alpikotopio"
				has_modifier = "class_chloerosmegagi"
				has_modifier = "class_chloeroslykofos"
				has_modifier = "class_adapted_terraformed"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_tropikostopio = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_ocean"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_archipelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_megalopelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_panpelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_ammoniapelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_okeanosgaean"
				has_modifier = "class_aquatic_terraformed"				
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_archipelagic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_tundra"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_cryotopio"
				has_modifier = "class_oreinos"
				has_modifier = "class_krystallomegagi"
				has_modifier = "class_adapted_terraformed"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_cryotopio = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_arctic"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_cryogenian"
				has_modifier = "class_pagosorimos"
				has_modifier = "class_cryomegagi"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_pagosorimos = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_planet_class = "pc_alpine"
			# Does not have one of the associated class modifiers:
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = "class_cryopelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_pagospelagic"
				has_modifier = "class_pagoslykofos"
				has_modifier = "class_aquatic_terraformed"
			}
		}
		# Remove any existing Biosphere modifier
		remove_biosphere_modifier = yes
		# Roll the default planet class
		roll_cryopelagic = yes
	}
}

## AUXILIAR EFFECTS

remove_uninhabitable_modifiers = { # And deposits and prevent anomalies as well - Used when converting an uninhabitable into a marginal
	clear_deposits = yes
	prevent_anomaly = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = ringed_planet }
		remove_modifier = ringed_planet
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = scorched_planetoid }
		remove_modifier = scorched_planetoid
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = stable_dual_moon_system }

## ATMOSPHERE SPAWN EFFECTS
## Logic:
## Atmospheres with variable water vapour should be more common on ideal stars
## Cold stars should favour carbon_poor
## Hot stars should favour carbon_rich
## Smaller worlds should give bonus to atmospheres with higher carbon ratio
## Larger worlds should give bonus to atmospheres with higher water vapour ratio
## Being a gas giant moon should increase volcanism, meaning more water vapour
## Having no parent nor moon should make for a less geoactive planet, less water vapour
## Modifiers below ordered from higher carbon ratio to lower, lower water vapour to higher
## Carbon poor, Volcanic, Ammonia, Sulfur and Artificial are manually spawned
## A base modifier of 0 means the scoped planet class should not be viable for that specific atmosphere because it doesn't have a proper biosphere for it

spawn_atmosphere-chloerosmegagi = {
	random_list = {
		0 = {
			modifier = { factor = 2.00 planet_size < 14 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size > 13 planet_size < 22 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 planet_size > 21 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 orbits_cold_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 orbits_ideal_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 orbits_hot_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 is_gas_giant_moon = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 NOT = { has_moon = yes is_moon = yes } }
			##
			modifier = { add = 1000 has_planet_flag = "has_carbon_rich_preference" } # This is used for Terraforming process
			modifier = { factor = 0.00 is_special_colony = yes } # This is important, homeworlds and guaranteed colonies should have a fixed atmosphere
			add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_rich" days = -1 }
		}
		20 = {
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 planet_size < 14 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size > 13 planet_size < 22 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 planet_size > 21 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 orbits_cold_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 orbits_ideal_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 orbits_hot_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 is_gas_giant_moon = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.25 NOT = { has_moon = yes is_moon = yes } }
			##
			modifier = { add = 1000 has_planet_flag = "has_oxygen_carbon_mix_preference" } # This is used for Terraforming process
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 is_special_colony = yes } # This is important, homeworlds and guaranteed colonies should have a fixed atmosphere
			add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix" days = -1 }
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size < 14 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size > 13 planet_size < 22 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size > 21 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 orbits_cold_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.25 orbits_ideal_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 orbits_hot_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 is_gas_giant_moon = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 NOT = { has_moon = yes is_moon = yes } }
			##
			modifier = { add = 1000 has_planet_flag = "has_lower_water_vapour_preference" } # This is used for Terraforming process
			modifier = { factor = 0.00 is_special_colony = yes } # This is important, homeworlds and guaranteed colonies should have a fixed atmosphere
			add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-lower_water_vapour" days = -1 }
		}
		10 = {
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 planet_size < 14 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size > 13 planet_size < 22 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 planet_size > 21 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 orbits_cold_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 orbits_ideal_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 orbits_hot_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.25 is_gas_giant_moon = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 NOT = { has_moon = yes is_moon = yes } }
			##
			modifier = { add = 1000 has_planet_flag = "has_variable_water_vapour_preference" } # This is used for Terraforming process
			modifier = { factor = 0.00 is_special_colony = yes } # This is important, homeworlds and guaranteed colonies should have a fixed atmosphere
			add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" days = -1 }
		}
		10 = {
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 planet_size < 14 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 planet_size > 13 planet_size < 22 }
			modifier = { factor = 2.00 planet_size > 21 }
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 orbits_cold_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 orbits_ideal_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 orbits_hot_star = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 is_gas_giant_moon = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.50 NOT = { has_moon = yes is_moon = yes } }
			##
			modifier = { add = 1000 has_planet_flag = "has_higher_water_vapour_preference" } # This is used for Terraforming process
			modifier = { factor = 0.00 is_special_colony = yes } # This is important, homeworlds and guaranteed colonies should have a fixed atmosphere
			add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-higher_water_vapour" days = -1 }
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 1000 has_planet_flag = "has_carbon_poor_preference" } # This is used for Terraforming process
			add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_poor" days = -1 }
		}
	}
}

spawn_atmosphere-algaemegagi = {
	random_list = {
		10 = {

correct_atmosphere_color = {
	# Lets use this to also re-order the modifiers in the event of some terraforming process
	# Planet class modifier always comes first
	# So we first remove the Atmosphere modifier only to spawn it again
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-variable_water_vapour }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-variable_water_vapour
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-lower_water_vapour }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-lower_water_vapour
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-lower_water_vapour" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-higher_water_vapour }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-higher_water_vapour
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-higher_water_vapour" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-carbon_poor }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-carbon_poor
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_poor" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-carbon_rich }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-carbon_rich
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_rich" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-ammonia_vapour }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-ammonia_vapour
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-ammonia_vapour" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-polluted }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-polluted
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-polluted" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-frigid_marginal }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-frigid_marginal
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-frigid_marginal" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-hot_marginal }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-hot_marginal
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-hot_marginal" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-wet_marginal }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-wet_marginal
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-wet_marginal" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-volcanic }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-volcanic
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-volcanic" days = -1 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-sulfuric_acid }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-sulfuric_acid
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-sulfuric_acid" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-methane }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-methane
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-methane" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-hothouse }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-hothouse
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-hothouse" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-desolate }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-desolate
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-desolate" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = atmosphere-artificial }
		remove_modifier = atmosphere-artificial
		add_modifier = { modifier = "atmosphere-artificial" days = -1 }
	}
	# Then the Biosphere
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-barren }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-barren
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-barren" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-tenuous }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-tenuous
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-tenuous" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-sparse }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-sparse
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-diverse }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-diverse
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-dense }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-dense
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-aquatic }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-aquatic
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-aquatic" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-ammonia }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-ammonia
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-ammonia" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-exotic }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-exotic
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-exotic" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-seeded }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-seeded
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-seeded" days = -1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = biosphere-engineered }
		remove_modifier = biosphere-engineered
		add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-engineered" days = -1 }
	}
	random_list = {
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 1 has_modifier = "atmosphere-artificial" }
			set_planet_entity = {
				atmosphere_color 		= hsv { 0.60 0.60 0.99 }
				atmosphere_intensity 	= 1.0
				atmosphere_width 		= 0.5
			}
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = { add = 1 has_modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" }
			set_planet_entity = {
				atmosphere_color 		= hsv { 0.59 0.45 0.95 }

	}

## BIOSPHERE SPAWN EFFECTS
## Logic:
## Each biosphere type will have a base chance of 0, a value will be added by modifier for each planet class that supports it
## This way we can use a single function that will work for every planet class
## Planet size and what type of star the planet orbits were already used as modifiers to spawn the atmosphere
## So for the biosphere, besides the planet class, the sole modifier will be the rolled Atmosphere
## Seeded, Aquatic, Ammonia and Engineered biospheres are manually spawned, as well as the ones for worlds that only support 1 type

spawn_biosphere = {
	random_list = {
		0 = {	# DENSE
			# Planet class base modifiers
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_megalopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_ipeirospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_pagospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_chloerosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_xirosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_pagosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_chloerosgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_retinalgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_thermogenian" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_cryogenian" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_mukesgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_cryotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_tropikostopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_thermotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_alpikotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_oreinos" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_savana" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_cryopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_thermopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_archipelagic" }
			# Atmosphere modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-higher_water_vapour" }	# IN PLANETS WITH LOTS OF WATER
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" }	# GOOD FOR DIVERSE BIOSPHERES
			modifier = { factor = 2.50 has_modifier = "atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix" }	# GOOD FOR LOTS OF TREES
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 has_modifier = "atmosphere-lower_water_vapour" }	# USUALLY FRIGID WHILE STILL ALLOWING VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 0.10 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_poor" }		# USUALLY FRIGID WITHOUT VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 0.10 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_rich" }		# USUALLY DRY WITH WEAK BIOSPHERES
			# Terraforming-related modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 0.01 has_planet_flag = "has_tenuous_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_planet_flag = "has_sparse_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 5.00 has_planet_flag = "has_diverse_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 10.00 has_planet_flag = "has_dense_preference" }
			##
			#add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-dense" days = -1 }
			set_planet_flag = "biosphere-dense"
		}
		0 = {	# DIVERSE
			# Planet class base modifiers
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_megalopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_ipeirospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_pagospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_chloerosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_xirosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_pagosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_chloerosgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_retinalgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_thermogenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_cryogenian" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_mukesgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_cryotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_tropikostopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_thermotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_alpikotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_oreinos" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_savana" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_cryopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_thermopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_archipelagic" }
			# Atmosphere modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = "atmosphere-higher_water_vapour" }	# IN PLANETS WITH LOTS OF WATER
			modifier = { factor = 2.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" }	# GOOD FOR DIVERSE BIOSPHERES
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = "atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix" }	# GOOD FOR LOTS OF TREES
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-lower_water_vapour" }	# USUALLY FRIGID WHILE STILL ALLOWING VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_poor" }		# USUALLY FRIGID WITHOUT VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_rich" }		# USUALLY DRY WITH WEAK BIOSPHERES
			# Terraforming-related modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 0.01 has_planet_flag = "has_tenuous_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_planet_flag = "has_sparse_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 10.00 has_planet_flag = "has_diverse_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 5.00 has_planet_flag = "has_dense_preference" }
			##
			#add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-diverse" days = -1 }
			set_planet_flag = "biosphere-diverse"
		}
		0 = {	# SPARSE
			# Planet class base modifiers
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_megalopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_ipeirospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_pagospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_chloerosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_xirosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_pagosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_chloerosgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_retinalgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_thermogenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_cryogenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_mukesgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_cryotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_tropikostopio" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_thermotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_alpikotopio" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_oreinos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_savana" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_cryopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_thermopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_archipelagic" }
			# Atmosphere modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-higher_water_vapour" }	# IN PLANETS WITH LOTS OF WATER
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" }	# GOOD FOR DIVERSE BIOSPHERES
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix" }	# GOOD FOR LOTS OF TREES
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = "atmosphere-lower_water_vapour" }	# USUALLY FRIGID WHILE STILL ALLOWING VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 0.25 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_poor" }		# USUALLY FRIGID WITHOUT VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_rich" }		# USUALLY DRY WITH WEAK BIOSPHERES
			# Terraforming-related modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 3.00 has_planet_flag = "has_tenuous_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 10.00 has_planet_flag = "has_sparse_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 2.00 has_planet_flag = "has_diverse_preference" }
			modifier = { factor = 0.01 has_planet_flag = "has_dense_preference" }
			##
			#add_modifier = { modifier = "biosphere-sparse" days = -1 }
			set_planet_flag = "biosphere-sparse"
		}
		0 = {	# TENUOUS
			# Planet class base modifiers
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_megalopelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_ipeirospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_pagospelagic" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_chloerosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_xirosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 10 has_modifier = "class_pagosorimos" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_chloerosgenian" }
			modifier = { add = 0 has_modifier = "class_retinalgenian" }

			# Atmosphere modifiers
			modifier = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-higher_water_vapour" }	# IN PLANETS WITH LOTS OF WATER
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 has_modifier = "atmosphere-variable_water_vapour" }	# GOOD FOR DIVERSE BIOSPHERES
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 has_modifier = "atmosphere-oxygen_carbon_mix" }	# GOOD FOR LOTS OF TREES

			modifier = { factor = 3.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_poor" }		# USUALLY FRIGID WITHOUT VEGETATION
			modifier = { factor = 4.00 has_modifier = "atmosphere-carbon_rich" }		# USUALLY DRY WITH WEAK BIOSPHERES
			# Terraforming-related modifiers

			modifier = { factor = 5.00 has_planet_flag = "has_sparse_preference" }

update_marginal_portrait = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = "class_hadean" }
		set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_hadean"
				entity = "primordial_hadean_01_entity"
				
			}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = "class_anthracean" }
		set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_anthracean"
				entity = "primordial_anthracean_01_entity"
				
			}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = "class_agonos" }
		set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_agonos"
				entity = "marginal_agonos_01_entity"
				
			}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = "class_hydrocarbonal" }
		set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_hydrocarbonal"
				entity = "sub_marginal_hydrocarbonal_01_entity"
				
			}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = "class_karstikos" }
		set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_karstikos"
				entity = "marginal_karstikos_01_entity"
				
			}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_modifier = "class_desolate" }
		set_planet_entity = {
				picture = "orbit_desolate"
				entity = "sub_marginal_desolate_01_entity"

	}
	if = {
